10.132.4.7       [37m+        item = reg.open(key)[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+        value = item[key_name] rescue nil[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+        next if value.nil?[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+        results.merge!("#{key.downcase}" => "#{value}")        [0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+      end[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+    end[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+    return results[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+  end[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+  # Does some regexing on the returned string from the registry in order to get the actual data we want (e.g. MAFAX87)[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+  def get_bccon_group[0m

10.132.4.7       [37m+    text = get_single_registry_key('SOFTWARE\Wow6432Node\SSTAI\Connector Container\Connectors\SapBCCONOut', 'Filter')[0m
